kubernetes/kubernetes repository:\\n\\n## CNI Plugin Invocation\\n\\nThe primary entry point for CNI execution is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go**, specifically the `createPodSandbox()` function (line 38). This function creates a PodSandboxConfig and calls `m.runtimeService.RunPodSandbox()` (line 68). This CRI gRPC call is delegated to the container runtime (containerd/CRI-O), which then invokes the appropriate CNI plugins based on the network configuration.\\n\\nThe pod sandbox configuration includes critical networking information set up by `generatePodSandboxConfig()` which includes DNS settings and references to the network namespace.\\n\\n## Network Namespace Setup\\n\\nNetwork namespace configuration for pods is handled in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/util/util.go** through the `NetworkNamespaceForPod()` function. This function is called during sandbox config generation to properly set up the network namespace path that will be used by CNI plugins to configure pod networking.\\n\\nLinux-specific namespace handling is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox_linux.go**, while Windows support is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox_windows.go**.\\n\\n## Network Setup Orchestration\\n\\nThe overall network setup orchestration happens at multiple levels:\\n\\n1. **Pod Worker Level** (pkg/kubelet/pod_workers.go): The pod worker's `SyncPod()` function coordinates the overall pod lifecycle\\n2. **Kubelet Network Level** (pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go): Contains `SetupPodNetwork()` and `TeardownPodNetwork()` functions that manage pod network setup/teardown\\n3. **Runtime Manager Level** (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go): The `SyncPod()` function orchestrates pod synchronization including sandbox creation\\n\\n## IP Address Management (IPAM)\\n\\nIPAM is handled by the Node IPAM Controller in **pkg/controller/nodeipam/node_ipam_controller.go**. This controller manages pod CIDR allocation on nodes. The actual CIDR allocation is performed through the `CIDRAllocator` interface defined in **pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/cidr_allocator.go**.\\n\\nThe IPAM controller allocates IP address ranges that are then used by CNI plugins to assign individual IPs to pods. The controller's `Run()` method continuously manages CIDR allocation for nodes in the cluster.\\n\\n## Sync Actions and Network State\\n\\nNetwork setup and teardown are tracked as sync actions in **pkg/kubelet/container/sync_result.go**, with constants `SetupNetwork` and `TeardownNetwork` indicating network operations during pod synchronization.\\n\\nNetwork readiness is tracked through the `NetworkReady` runtime condition in **pkg/kubelet/container/runtime.go**, which indicates whether the container runtime's network is ready to accept pods.\\n\\n## DNS Configuration\\n\\nDNS configuration for pods is handled separately in **pkg/kubelet/network/dns/dns.go** (cross-platform), **pkg/kubelet/network/dns/dns_windows.go** (Windows), and is also part of the sandbox config generation.\\n\\n## Monitoring and Metrics\\n\\nThe startup latency of the first network pod is tracked in **pkg/kubelet/metrics/metrics.go** through `FirstNetworkPodStartSLIDuration` metric, helping identify CNI plugin performance issues. Pod startup latency tracking is implemented in **pkg/kubelet/util/pod_startup_latency_tracker.go**.\\n\\n## Summary of CNI Integration Flow\\n\\n1. Pod worker calls Kubelet's SetupPodNetwork()\\n2. Kubelet delegates to KubeRuntime manager's SyncPod()\\n3. createPodSandbox() generates PodSandboxConfig with network namespace via generatePodSandboxConfig()\\n4. NetworkNamespaceForPod() sets up the network namespace path\\n5. RunPodSandbox() CRI call is made to container runtime\\n6. Container runtime (containerd/CRI-O) invokes CNI plugins\\n7. IPAM controller has previously allocated CIDR ranges for the node\\n8. CNI plugins use allocated CIDR ranges to assign IPs to pod interfaces\\n9. Network setup is tracked through sync actions (SetupNetwork/TeardownNetwork)\\n10. Network readiness is checked before allowing pod execution\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3032,"cache_read_input_tokens":76239,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3032},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"059c2366-c993-4339-a543-08eac039558d","uuid":"bdee31d9-2f24-4e39-9e1d-e21b04939f6d"}

\"description\": \"IPAM allocates CIDR ranges for pods on nodes\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes CNI (Container Network Interface) integration is implemented across multiple layers in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository:\\n\\n## CNI Plugin Invocation\\n\\nThe primary entry point for CNI execution is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go**, specifically the `createPodSandbox()` function (line 38). This function creates a PodSandboxConfig and calls `m.runtimeService.RunPodSandbox()` (line 68). This CRI gRPC call is delegated to the container runtime (containerd/CRI-O), which then invokes the appropriate CNI plugins based on the network configuration.\\n\\nThe pod sandbox configuration includes critical networking information set up by `generatePodSandboxConfig()` which includes DNS settings and references to the network namespace.\\n\\n## Network Namespace Setup\\n\\nNetwork namespace configuration for pods is handled in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/util/util.go** through the `NetworkNamespaceForPod()` function. This function is called during sandbox config generation to properly set up the network namespace path that will be used by CNI plugins to configure pod networking.\\n\\nLinux-specific namespace handling is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox_linux.go**, while Windows support is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox_windows.go**.\\n\\n## Network Setup Orchestration\\n\\nThe overall network setup orchestration happens at multiple levels:\\n\\n1. **Pod Worker Level** (pkg/kubelet/pod_workers.go): The pod worker's `SyncPod()` function coordinates the overall pod lifecycle\\n2. **Kubelet Network Level** (pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go): Contains `SetupPodNetwork()` and `TeardownPodNetwork()` functions that manage pod network setup/teardown\\n3. **Runtime Manager Level** (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go): The `SyncPod()` function orchestrates pod synchronization including sandbox creation\\n\\n## IP Address Management (IPAM)\\n\\nIPAM is handled by the Node IPAM Controller in **pkg/controller/nodeipam/node_ipam_controller.go**. This controller manages pod CIDR allocation on nodes. The actual CIDR allocation is performed through the `CIDRAllocator` interface defined in **pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/cidr_allocator.go**.\\n\\nThe IPAM controller allocates IP address ranges that are then used by CNI plugins to assign individual IPs to pods. The controller's `Run()` method continuously manages CIDR allocation for nodes in the cluster.\\n\\n## Sync Actions and Network State\\n\\nNetwork setup and teardown are tracked as sync actions in **pkg/kubelet/container/sync_result.go**, with constants `SetupNetwork` and `TeardownNetwork` indicating network operations during pod synchronization.\\n\\nNetwork readiness is tracked through the `NetworkReady` runtime condition in **pkg/kubelet/container/runtime.go**, which indicates whether the container runtime's network is ready to accept pods.\\n\\n## DNS Configuration\\n\\nDNS configuration for pods is handled separately in **pkg/kubelet/network/dns/dns.go** (cross-platform), **pkg/kubelet/network/dns/dns_windows.go** (Windows), and is also part of the sandbox config generation.\\n\\n## Monitoring and Metrics\\n\\nThe startup latency of the first network pod is tracked in **pkg/kubelet/metrics/metrics.go** through `FirstNetworkPodStartSLIDuration` metric, helping identify CNI plugin performance issues. Pod startup latency tracking is implemented in **pkg/kubelet/util/pod_startup_latency_tracker.go**.\\n\\n## Summary of CNI Integration Flow\\n\\n1. Pod worker calls Kubelet's SetupPodNetwork()\\n2. Kubelet delegates to KubeRuntime manager's SyncPod()\\n3. createPodSandbox() generates PodSandboxConfig with network namespace via generatePodSandboxConfig()\\n4. NetworkNamespaceForPod() sets up the network namespace path\\n5. RunPodSandbox() CRI call is made to container runtime\\n6. Container runtime (containerd/CRI-O) invokes CNI plugins\\n7. IPAM controller has previously allocated CIDR ranges for the node\\n8. CNI plugins use allocated CIDR ranges to assign IPs to pod interfaces\\n9. Network setup is tracked through sync actions (SetupNetwork/TeardownNetwork)\\n10. Network readiness is checked before allowing pod execution\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

(Container Network Interface) integration is implemented across multiple layers in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository:\\n\\n## CNI Plugin Invocation\\n\\nThe primary entry point for CNI execution is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go**, specifically the `createPodSandbox()` function (line 38). This function creates a PodSandboxConfig and calls `m.runtimeService.RunPodSandbox()` (line 68). This CRI gRPC call is delegated to the container runtime (containerd/CRI-O), which then invokes the appropriate CNI plugins based on the network configuration.\\n\\nThe pod sandbox configuration includes critical networking information set up by `generatePodSandboxConfig()` which includes DNS settings and references to the network namespace.\\n\\n## Network Namespace Setup\\n\\nNetwork namespace configuration for pods is handled in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/util/util.go** through the `NetworkNamespaceForPod()` function. This function is called during sandbox config generation to properly set up the network namespace path that will be used by CNI plugins to configure pod networking.\\n\\nLinux-specific namespace handling is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox_linux.go**, while Windows support is in **pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox_windows.go**.\\n\\n## Network Setup Orchestration\\n\\nThe overall network setup orchestration happens at multiple levels:\\n\\n1. **Pod Worker Level** (pkg/kubelet/pod_workers.go): The pod worker's `SyncPod()` function coordinates the overall pod lifecycle\\n2. **Kubelet Network Level** (pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go): Contains `SetupPodNetwork()` and `TeardownPodNetwork()` functions that manage pod network setup/teardown\\n3. **Runtime Manager Level** (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go): The `SyncPod()` function orchestrates pod synchronization including sandbox creation\\n\\n## IP Address Management (IPAM)\\n\\nIPAM is handled by the Node IPAM Controller in **pkg/controller/nodeipam/node_ipam_controller.go**. This controller manages pod CIDR allocation on nodes. The actual CIDR allocation is performed through the `CIDRAllocator` interface defined in **pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/cidr_allocator.go**.\\n\\nThe IPAM controller allocates IP address ranges that are then used by CNI plugins to assign individual IPs to pods. The controller's `Run()` method continuously manages CIDR allocation for nodes in the cluster.\\n\\n## Sync Actions and Network State\\n\\nNetwork setup and teardown are tracked as sync actions in **pkg/kubelet/container/sync_result.go**, with constants `SetupNetwork` and `TeardownNetwork` indicating network operations during pod synchronization.\\n\\nNetwork readiness is tracked through the `NetworkReady` runtime condition in **pkg/kubelet/container/runtime.go**, which indicates whether the container runtime's network is ready to accept pods.\\n\\n## DNS Configuration\\n\\nDNS configuration for pods is handled separately in **pkg/kubelet/network/dns/dns.go** (cross-platform), **pkg/kubelet/network/dns/dns_windows.go** (Windows), and is also part of the sandbox config generation.\\n\\n## Monitoring and Metrics\\n\\nThe startup latency of the first network pod is tracked in **pkg/kubelet/metrics/metrics.go** through `FirstNetworkPodStartSLIDuration` metric, helping identify CNI plugin performance issues. Pod startup latency tracking is implemented in **pkg/kubelet/util/pod_startup_latency_tracker.go**.\\n\\n## Summary of CNI Integration Flow\\n\\n1. Pod worker calls Kubelet's SetupPodNetwork()\\n2. Kubelet delegates to KubeRuntime manager's SyncPod()\\n3. createPodSandbox() generates PodSandboxConfig with network namespace via generatePodSandboxConfig()\\n4. NetworkNamespaceForPod() sets up the network namespace path\\n5. RunPodSandbox() CRI call is made to container runtime\\n6. Container runtime (containerd/CRI-O) invokes CNI plugins\\n7. IPAM controller has previously allocated CIDR ranges for the node\\n8. CNI plugins use allocated CIDR ranges to assign IPs to pod interfaces\\n9. Network setup is tracked through sync actions (SetupNetwork/TeardownNetwork)\\n10. Network readiness is checked before allowing pod execution\"\n   287→}\n   288→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
